(I put a few beautiful photos of Tianjin that I took casually while shopping, I don‚Äôt know how to take pictures, let‚Äôs take a lookü§≠)
advantage:
1. The traffic is very convenient. It‚Äôs pretty good. To go to a scenic spot like Jinwan Square, make an appoin**ent with Didi first. I booked an express train from Baiyun Hotel to Exit B of Airport Subway Station. It‚Äôs about 13-16 (it may be more expensive when you come back at night. It‚Äôs 19, it‚Äôs okay.) Then take Line 3 to Tianjin Station, and transfer to Line 2 if you go to other scenic spots.
2. The hotel room is very large and clean. The bedding was not stained. The water in the bathing pool is not yellow and cloudy. There are 2 beds, 2 small sofas (single) and TV in the room; the bathroom has a bathtub, shower room, toilet, and washstand.
3. The elevators in the hotel are very clean, bright and tidy, and the elevators are equipped with disposable disinfectant. Call an elevator and press a button, and the others will light up together, so there will be no situation where you go to the four elevator buttons and press one by one to light up. This is very convenient.
4. The lobby has a faint fragrance, bright and tidy, and the check-in is very efficient and fast. I was number two in line. During the queue, a little brother asked me if I wanted to carry my bag. The service is very good, nothing to sayüëç.

shortcoming:
1. The light has a row of switches, and one of the switches does not work very well. When the switch is pressed, the light does not turn on, and the other lights are normally on.
2. The carpet was dirty. I dropped a white thing and picked it up with a bunch of small black spots on it. There is rubbish under the TV cabinet, there is something like a rotten grape or a lychee core.
3. The TV channel is not very clear and there are snowflakes.
I mainly come to Tianjin to play, play a full day during the day, and come to save a night at night, so these shortcomings can be ignored haha ‚Äã‚Äãü§î. Personally, I feel that the hotel is very cost-effective, the price is not expensive, and the transportation is very convenient.
